2013 Jul 23  13:30:12.113  [00]  0xB0C0  LTE RRC OTA Packet  --  BCCH_DL_SCH
Pkt Version = 2
RRC Release Number.Major.minor = 9.10.0
Radio Bearer ID = 0, Physical Cell ID = 164

SysFrameNum = 570, SubFrameNum = 5
PDU Number = BCCH_DL_SCH Message,    Msg Length = 18

Interpreted PDU:

value BCCH-DL-SCH-Message ::= 
{
  message c1 : systemInformationBlockType1 : 
      {
        cellAccessRelatedInfo 
        {
          plmn-IdentityList 
          {
            {
              plmn-Identity 
              {
                mcc 												;China
                {
                  4,
                  6,
                  0
                },
                mnc 												;China Mobile(CMCC)
                {
                  0,
                  0
                }
              },
              cellReservedForOperatorUse notReserved
            }
          },
          trackingAreaCode '00000000 00110010'B,						;TAI: 0d50, 0x32
          cellIdentity '10101101 01110001 00010000 0011'B,					;ECI, E-UTRAN Cell Identifier, identify a cell within a PLMN
          cellBarred notBarred,
          intraFreqReselection allowed,
          csg-Indication FALSE
        },
        cellSelectionInfo 
        {
          q-RxLevMin -64												;Qrxlevmin = -64*2 = -128 dBm, RSRP
        },
        freqBandIndicator 39,											; band 39, F, 1880~1900MHz (*1900~1920 is used by PHS)
        schedulingInfoList 												;Scheduling info for other SI. SIB2 is always the Default and first, which is common radio resource info.
        {
          {
            si-Periodicity rf16,
            sib-MappingInfo 
            {
              sibType3												; cell re-selection info (common, i.e. for more than 1 type).
            }
          },
          {
            si-Periodicity rf32,
            sib-MappingInfo 
            {
              sibType5
            }
          }
        },
        tdd-Config 
        {
          subframeAssignment sa2,									;number of DL/UP frames: 3/1
          specialSubframePatterns ssp6								;DwPTS:GP:UpUps 9:3:2
        },
        si-WindowLength ms40,
        systemInfoValueTag 3										;0~31
      }
}

SI scheduling:
SIB1 is decoded in SFN=570. 
570%8=1 =>it’s the 2nd transmission in its 80ms period.

SIB2,3: 		Si-windowLength 40ms,            si-Periodicity rf16,
570/16=35.625. 1st si-Periodicity=rf16 =>the 1st SI will be in a 40ms window from SFN=576=36*16. It’s for SIB2,3
sibType5: 	the 2nd si-periodicity=rf32 => is from SFN=18*32+4=580

SFN, System Frame Number, 0~1023

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
TC1.11, the same scheduling, in bad radio condition, 1st SIB1 is at SFN 988, 1st SI is at SFN 99; SIB5 is at SFN101. There’s 135RF=1.35s delay. 
SI window start SFN: 16*6=96. 	32*3+4=100.

value BCCH-DL-SCH-Message ::= 
{
  message c1 : systemInformation : 
      {
        criticalExtensions systemInformation-r8 : 
          {
            sib-TypeAndInfo 
            {
              sib2 : 
                {
                  radioResourceConfigCommon 
                  {
                    rach-ConfigCommon 
                    {
                      preambleInfo 
                      {
                        numberOfRA-Preambles n52,					; Number of non-dedicated random access preamble, 52/64
                        preamblesGroupAConfig 					;Group A: msg3 is small and path loss is big, TS 36.321
                        {
                          sizeOfRA-PreamblesGroupA n28,
                          messageSizeGroupA b56,
                          messagePowerOffsetGroupB dB10			;compare(PL, PCMAX, c-preambleInitialReceivedTargetPower-deltaPreambleMsg3-messagePowerOffsetGroupB)
                        }
                      },
                      powerRampingParameters 
                      {
                        powerRampingStep dB2,
                        preambleInitialReceivedTargetPower dBm-104			;-120~-90dBm(Step 2). Delta_preamble_4=8dB
                      },
                      ra-SupervisionInfo 
                      {
                        preambleTransMax n10,
                        ra-ResponseWindowSize sf10,				;RAR is monitored in 10 subframes from 3 subframes after the RA ending
                        mac-ContentionResolutionTimer sf64			;wait msg4 from msg3
                      },
                      maxHARQ-Msg3Tx 5
                    },
                    bcch-Config 
                    {
                      modificationPeriodCoeff n2					; modification period (in rf)= modificationPeriodCoeff * defaultPagingCycle
                    },
                    pcch-Config 
                    {
                      defaultPagingCycle rf128,
                      nB oneT
                    },
                    prach-Config 
                    {
                      rootSequenceIndex 104,
                      prach-ConfigInfo 
                      {
                        prach-ConfigIndex 53,					; TS 36.211 [5.7.1, table5.7.1-4],  RA f&t resource (*in UpPTS)
                        highSpeedFlag FALSE,
                        zeroCorrelationZoneConfig 6,				; TS 36.211, [ 5.7.2: table 5.7.2-3], Ncd, to define cyclic shift
                        prach-FreqOffset 0
                      }
                    },
                    pdsch-ConfigCommon 
                    {
                      referenceSignalPower 10,					; downlink reference-signal EPRE, see TS 36.213 [ 5.2], dBm
                      p-b 0									; TS 36.213 [Table 5.2-1], ->the power ratio of with and without CRS symbols. 0 -> 1 for 1ant, 5/4 for 2or4 ant
                    },
                    pusch-ConfigCommon 
                    {
                      pusch-ConfigBasic 
                      {
                        n-SB 4,								; TS 36.211 [ 5.3.4], number of sub-bands for hopping
                        hoppingMode interSubFrame,
                        pusch-HoppingOffset 25,				; , to get the predefined hopping pattern
                        enable64QAM TRUE
                      },
                      ul-ReferenceSignalsPUSCH 				; 
                      {
                        groupHoppingEnabled FALSE,				; 36.211 [ 5.5.1.3] . The sequence-group number u in slot ns is defined by a PN group hopping pattern fgh(ns) and a sequence-shift pattern fss
                        groupAssignmentPUSCH 0,				; for fss and delta-ss
                        sequenceHoppingEnabled FALSE,
                        cyclicShift 0							;mapping to , 36.211[5.5.2.1.1]
                      }
                    },
                    pucch-ConfigCommon 
                    {
                      deltaPUCCH-Shift ds1,				; , pucch sequence cyclic shifter interval, 36.211 [5.4.1], related to the resource number of PUCCH format 1/1a/1b
                      nRB-CQI 1,						; , TS 36.211 [ 5.4], RB number for PUCCH formats 2/2a/2b tx in each slot
                      nCS-AN 0,						; , the number of cyclic shift used for PUCCH formats 1/1a/1b in a RB used for mix formats 1&2
                      n1PUCCH-AN 10					; , see TS 36.213 [10.1], AN shift(based on n-cce)
                    },
                    soundingRS-UL-ConfigCommon setup : 
                      {
                        srs-BandwidthConfig bw2,		; cell-specific parameter srs-BandwidthConfig, , TS36.211[5.5.3.2], depend on UL-BW,

                        ackNackSRS-SimultaneousTransmission TRUE,	; TS 36.213 [ 8.2]
                        srs-MaxUpPts true				;  applies for UpPts, , where  is a SRS BW configuration
                      },
                    uplinkPowerControlCommon 
                    {
                      p0-NominalPUSCH -67,			; , TS 36.213[ 5.1.1.1], -126dBm~24
                      alpha al07,						; 36.213 [ 5.1.1.1], 0.7 partial compensation for PL(PUSCH)
                      p0-NominalPUCCH -105,			; , TS 36.213, 5.1.2.1, (-127..-96)dBm
                      deltaFList-PUCCH 				; , See TS 36.213 [5.1.2], to set UE transmit power
                      {
                        deltaF-PUCCH-Format1 deltaF0,		;for Scheduling Request
                        deltaF-PUCCH-Format1b deltaF3,		;for 2b ACK/NACK,QPSK; 3dB, relative to PUCCH format 1a(for 1b ACK/NACK)
                        deltaF-PUCCH-Format2 deltaF1,		;for CQI(20b)
                        deltaF-PUCCH-Format2a deltaF2,		;for CQI+ACK/NACK(1b)
                        deltaF-PUCCH-Format2b deltaF2		;for CQI+ACK/NACK(2b)
                      },
                      deltaPreambleMsg3 6				; , TS 36.213 [ 5.1.1.1] <= *2
                    },
                    ul-CyclicPrefixLength len1			; normal cyclic prefix
                  },
                  ue-TimersAndConstants 
                  {
                    t300 ms1000,				; rrcConnectionRequest->
                    t301 ms1000,				;rrcConnectionReestabilishmentRequest->
                    t310 ms2000,				;physical layer problems N310 out-of-sync->
                    n310 n10,
                    t311 ms10000,			;init rrc Connection reestablish ->, defaut ms1000
                    n311 n1					;in-sync
                  },
                  freqInfo 
                  {
                    additionalSpectrumEmission 1		; TS 36.101 [table 6.2.4.1], Additional Maximum Power Reduction (A-MPR), NA, 频谱模板
                  },
                  timeAlignmentTimerCommon sf1920	; how long the UE is considered uplink time aligned.
                },
              sib3 : 
                {
                  cellReselectionInfoCommon 
                  {
                    q-Hyst dB4,						；hysteresis value for ranking criteria
                    speedStateReselectionPars 
                    {
                      mobilityStateParameters 
                      {
                        t-Evaluation s60,
                        t-HystNormal s30,			; The additional duration for evaluating criteria to enter normal mobility state. Corresponds to TCRmaxHyst in TS 36.304
                        n-CellChangeMedium 4,
                        n-CellChangeHigh 8
                      },
                      q-HystSF 			;speed dependent scalingfactor for Qhyst
                      {
                        sf-Medium dB0,
                        sf-High dB0
                      }
                    }
                  },
                  cellReselectionServingFreqInfo 
                  {
                    s-NonIntraSearch 0,		;reselction threshold <= *2
                    threshServingLow 10,		;ThreshServing, LowP, if serving cell RSRP is lower than this threshold, consider the lower priority frequency
                    cellReselectionPriority 7		;highest
                  },
                  intraFreqCellReselectionInfo 
                  {
                    q-RxLevMin -64,
                    s-IntraSearch 29,				; SIntraSearchP, db, if Srxlev< s-IntraSearch, do intra search
                    presenceAntennaPort1 FALSE,	; whether all the neighbouring cells use Antenna Port 1
                    neighCellConfig '01'B,			; No MBSFN subframes are present in all neighbour cells; same UL/DL allocation
                    t-ReselectionEUTRA 1,			; TreselectionEUTRA, time interval, (0~7)seconds
                    t-ReselectionEUTRA-SF 
                    {
                      sf-Medium lDot0,		;1.0
                      sf-High oDot75
                    }

                  {
                    s-IntraSearchP-r9 29,			;use it instead of s-IntraSearch, RSRP
                    s-IntraSearchQ-r9 5			;RSRQ

                  {
                    s-NonIntraSearchP-r9 0,
                    s-NonIntraSearchQ-r9 4
                  },
                  q-QualMin-r9 -18			; Qqualmin, dB, cell selection/ re-selection the required minimum received RSRQ, (-34..-3)
                }
            }
          }
      }

RACH
Comment
TS36.300[10.1.5]
The random access procedure is performed for the following events related to the PCell:
-	Initial access from RRC_IDLE;
-	RRC Connection Re-establishment procedure;
-	Handover;
-	DL data arrival during RRC_CONNECTED requiring random access procedure;
-	E.g. when UL synchronisation status is “non-synchronised”;
-	UL data arrival during RRC_CONNECTED requiring random access procedure;
-	E.g. when UL synchronisation status is "non-synchronised" or there are no PUCCH resources for SR available.
-	For positioning purpose during RRC_CONNECTED requiring random access procedure;
-	E.g. when timing advance is needed for UE positioning;
The random access procedure is also performed on a SCell to establish time alignment for the corresponding sTAG.
Furthermore, the random access procedure takes two distinct forms:
-	Contention based (applicable to first five events);
-	Non-contention based (applicable to only handover, DL data arrival, positioning and obtaining timing advance alignment for a sTAG).
Normal DL/UL transmission can take place after the random access procedure.

Attach
TC
1.1.1~6 TD-LTE attach	
Hit rate and time consuming 		condition: weak/middle/good
Comment：
Just use the weak/middle/good point in test specification.

Weak*
middle
good
SINR(dB)
-5~0
5~10
15~20
* Suggested SINR(dB) -3~0, Suggested RSRP(dBm) <-100.

A(band34， 2010~2025MHz)， F频段（band39， 1880～1920M）、E频段（band40，2300～2400M，目前已分配2320～2370M）和D频段（band38， 2570～2620M）

TS36.101 
8.1.1 

Where the superscript indicates the receiver antenna connector.

8.4.2.1 Demodulation of PDCCH, TDD, Single-antenna port performance
Probability of miss-detection of the Downlink Scheduling Grant (Pm-dsg)
10MHz 8CCE : SNR（-1.6dB）, Pm-dsg（1%）


The printed SINR in log is inside the UE. The calculation is unknown to users. It includes receiver noise, PDCCH adaption, HARQ etc. considerations.
CQI 1: QPSK, code rate(78/1024), SNR (-6.71dB), BLER(0.1)

Signaling:


Ex:
1. BCCH: SIB1; SIB2, SIB3; camped
2. EMM: Attach Request
a) UL_CCCH: rrcConnectionRequest
b) DL_CCCH: rrcConnectionSetup
c) UL_DCCH: rrcConnectionSetupComplete (NAS info here!)
3. Authentication
a) DL-DCCH: dlInformationTransfer + EMM: Authentication Request
b) UL-DCCH: ulInformationTransfer + EMM: Authentication Response
4. Security Mode
a) DL-DCCH: dlInformationTransfer + EMM: Security mode command	
b) UL-DCCH: ulInformationTransfer + EMM: Security Mode Complete
5. ESM Information Request/response 
a) DL-DCCH: dlInformationTransfer + ESM Information Request
b) UL-DCCH: ulInformationTransfer + ESM Information response
: access_point_name
6. Ue Capability
a) DL-DCCH: Ue CapabilityEnquiry
b) UL-DCCH: ueCapabilityInformation
7. SecurityModeCommand (AS)
8. rrcConnectionReconfiguration + EMM: Attach Accept + ESM: Activate default EPS bearer context request
9. ulInformationTransfer + EMM: Attach complete + ESM: Activate default EPS bearer context accept
10. rrcConnectionReconfiguration: radioResourceConfigDedicated: physicalConfigDedicated：transmissionMode tm3
…
11. rrcConnectionRelease

lte_emm_msg
TAU
Comment
TS24.301[5.5.3]
The tracking area updating procedure is always initiated by the UE and is used for the following purposes:
-	normal tracking area updating to update the registration of the actual tracking area of a UE in the network;
-	combined tracking area updating to update the registration of the actual tracking area for a UE in CS/PS mode 1 or CS/PS mode 2 of operation;
-	periodic tracking area updating to periodically notify the availability of the UE to the network;
-	IMSI attach for non-EPS services when the UE is attached for EPS services. This procedure is used by a UE in CS/PS mode 1 or CS/PS mode 2 of operation;
-	in various cases of inter-system change from Iu mode to S1 mode or from A/Gb mode to S1 mode;
-	S101 mode to S1 mode inter-system change;
-	MME load balancing;
-	to update certain UE specific parameters in the network;
-	recovery from certain error cases;
-	to indicate that the UE enters S1 mode after CS fallback or 1xCS fallback;
-	to indicate to the network that the UE has selected a CSG cell whose CSG identity and associated PLMN identity are not included in the UE's Allowed CSG list or in the UE's Operator CSG list;
-	to indicate the current radio access technology to the network for the support of terminating access domain selection for voice calls or voice sessions; and
-	to indicate to the network that the UE has locally released EPS bearer context(s).

TD-LTE service setup 
Comment
TC 2.2.2
Signaling
1. EMM: Service Request
a) rrcConnectionSetupRequest(mo-Data)/Setup/Complete

TD-LTE 1.2.1
Comment
In tc1.2.1 Log: It’s a complicated log.

UE is implicitly detached when it’s back to LTE.
2 PDN connectivities are setup. eps bearer 5 -> cmnet; 6->cmwap
Signaling
1. BCCH: SIB1
2. Tracking Area Update Request
a) UL_CCCH: rrcConnectionRequest
b) DL_CCCH: rrcConnectionSetup
c) UL_DCCH:rrcConnectionSetupComplete (piggy NAS)
3. Tracking Area Updae Reject
a) DL_CCCH: rrcConnectionSetup
b) DL_DCCH: dlInformationTransfer (piggy NAS)
c) DL_DCCH: rrcConnectionRelease

4. Attach Request/Accept(act default eps_bearer, id5)/Complete[245622]

5. rrcConnectionReconfiguration
a) radioResourceConfigDedicated: physicalConfigDedicated
6. PDN connectivity request
7. Activate default EPS bearer context request/ accept (eps_bearer_id = 6)
a) rrcConnectionReconfiguration（+drb2）[277672]
b) ulInformationTransfer 

8. ulInformationTransfer ＋　PDN disconnect request(eps_bearer_id = 6)
9. dlInformationTransfer ＋Deactivate EPS bearer context request
10. rrcConnectionReconfiguration（-drb2）
11. ulInformationTransfer　＋　Deactivate EPS bearer context request　 accept
12. rrcConnectionRelease

value SysInfoType3 ::= 
{
  sib4indicator FALSE,
  cellIdentity '01100000 10010010 01001111 1011'B,
  cellSelectReselectInfo 
  {
    cellSelectQualityMeasure cpich-RSCP : NULL,
    modeSpecificInfo tdd : 
      {
        s-Intrasearch 21,				; *2+1=dB!当TD主小区的S值小于等于Sintrasearch时，就要执行同频小区重选测量. Srxlev根据P-CCPCH的接收功率等计算得到
        s-Intersearch 21,
        rat-List 
        {
          {
            rat-Identifier gsm,
            s-SearchRAT 0,			;-105~91dB(13, 0*2+1=1dB) 如果Srxlev小于等于Ssearch,RAT开始进行RAT间邻区测量
            s-Limit-SearchRAT 0
          }
        },
        q-RxlevMin -53			; 小区选择S准则, -115~-25dBm(-103, -53*2+1=-105), step 2.
      },
    q-Hyst-l-S 2,					;0~40dB, (4, 2dB)
    t-Reselection-S 2,				; 0~31seconds(2, 2s)
    maxAllowedUL-TX-Power 24
  },
  cellAccessRestriction 
  {
    cellBarred notBarred : NULL,
    cellReservedForOperatorUse notReserved,

Protocol error, unspecified










Any other value received by the mobile station shall be treated as 0110 1111, "Protocol error, unspecified". Any other value received by the network shall be treated as 0110 1111, "Protocol error, unspecified".

NOTE:	The listed reject cause values are defined in annex G.


GERAN
SI
A SI is sent in segments. 
1）、系统消息类型1：小区信道的描述+RACH控制参数。
2）、系统消息类型2：邻小区BCCH频点描述+RACH控制消息+允许的PLMN。
3）、系统消息类型2bis：扩展邻小区BCCH频点描述+RACH控制消息。
4）、系统消息类型2ter：扩展邻小区BCCH频点描述2。
4a) 系统消息类型2quater: 3G 4G邻小区信息
5）、系统消息类型3：小区识别（CELLID）+位置区识别(LAI)+控制信道描述+小区选择+小区选择参数+RACH控制参数。
6）、系统消息类型4：位置区识别+小区选择参数+RACH控制参数+CBCH信道描述+CBCH移动配置。
7）、系统消息类型5：邻小区BCCH频点的描述。
8）、系统消息类型5bis: 扩展邻近小区BCCH频点描述。（不同频段间的bcch描述，例如gsm900与dcs1800间handover request）。
9）、系统消息类型5ter: 扩展邻近小区BCCH频点描述。
10）、系统消息类型6:小区识别+位置区识别+小区选择。
11）、系统消息类型7：小区重选参数：
12）、系统消息类型8：小区重选参数：

DISCONNECT
原因(CAUSE VALUE)
用户感受
被叫TCH拥塞
34: No circurt/channel available
录音通知,暂时无法接通
主叫TCH拥塞
34: No circurt/channel available 
连续的嘟嘟嘟嘟
有寻呼消息,但没有PAGING_RESPONSE 
16: normal clearing
录音通知,暂时无法接通
被叫SDCCH拥塞
16: normal clearing
录音通知,暂时无法接通
主叫SDCCH拥塞 
没有DISCONNECT 消息
没有任何提示音,直接返回
SDCCH 掉话
41：temp failure
录音通知,暂时无法接通
错误号码
28：Invalid number format
主叫在听到一阵杂音后，多来米
呼叫无应答
18: alerting,but no answe
录音通知,用户无人接听
CIC 复位
111：protocol error
主叫听见多来米
被叫位置更新
41：temp failure
录音通知,暂时无法接通
连接超时
102
主叫听见多来米，被叫无寻呼信息
